# Monster & Combat NPC Catalogue (HighFive)

## Overview

Every combat-relevant NPC the client can target, drawn from the L2JMobius server's `dist/game/data/stats/npcs/*.xml`. Scope:

- **Monsters** — regular mobs (`type="Monster"` / `L2Monster`).
- **Bosses** — `RaidBoss`, `GrandBoss`.
- **Specials** — festival monsters, rift invaders, feedable / tamed beasts, chests.
- **Combat NPCs** — guards, defenders, fort commanders, quest guards, decoys, friendly mobs.

Excluded: merchants, teleporters, trainers, warehouse keepers, doormen, village masters, clan hall / fort managers, pets, summons, effect points, static towers, territory wards. None of those ever appear as an attack target.

- **Regenerate with:** `python scripts/gen_mobs_doc.py`. Output is deterministic.
- **Related:** packet-level combat flow — see [PROTOCOL.md](PROTOCOL.md). Skills referenced by `Skills` column — see [SKILLS.md](SKILLS.md). Item ids in drop/spoil tables — see [ITEMS.md](ITEMS.md).

### Column meanings

| Column | Meaning |
|--------|---------|
| **Id** | `npcId` on the wire (`NpcInfo 0x16`, `AttackableDeath`, etc.). |
| **Name** | Display name as shipped in the XML. Entries with `usingServerSideName=true` pull their name from the client's own `.dat` and may be empty here. |
| **Lv** | Level (unsigned). |
| **Race** | From `Race.java` enum (HUMAN, UNDEAD, DEMONIC, DRAGON, BEAST, …). |
| **HP** | Max HP at full health (integer-truncated from the decimal in XML). |
| **pAtk / mAtk** | Physical / magical attack from `<stats><attack>`. |
| **pDef / mDef** | Physical / magical defence from `<stats><defence>`. |
| **Rng** | Physical attack range (melee ≈ 40, bow ≈ 500+). |
| **Exp / SP** | Awarded to the killing party on death. |
| **Aggro** | `<ai aggroRange>` — radius at which the mob pulls unprovoked. Blank = non-aggressive. |
| **Skills** | Count of `<skillList><skill>` entries (includes passives & racial skills). |
| **Drops** | Count of `<drop>` item entries; `+Ns` suffix = N spoil items. |

## Summary counts

| Type | Count |
|------|---:|
| `GrandBoss` — Grand Bosses | 26 |
| `RaidBoss` — Raid Bosses | 344 |
| `Monster` — Monsters | 3795 |
| `L2Monster` — Monsters (legacy `L2Monster` tag) | 1 |
| `FestivalMonster` — Festival monsters | 110 |
| `RiftInvader` — Rift invaders | 132 |
| `FeedableBeast` — Feedable beasts | 91 |
| `TamedBeast` — Tamed beasts | 10 |
| `Chest` — Chests | 77 |
| `Guard` — Guards | 182 |
| `Defender` — Defenders | 633 |
| `FortCommander` — Fort commanders | 75 |
| `QuestGuard` — Quest guards | 12 |
| `FriendlyMob` — Friendly mobs | 5 |
| `Decoy` — Decoys | 17 |
| **Total** | **5510** |

## Boss drop detail

Per-mob drop + spoil listings for RaidBoss and GrandBoss only. `Group %` is the drop-group roll chance — the per-item `Chance %` is conditional on the group rolling. For regular monsters, read the source XML (`dist/game/data/stats/npcs/*.xml`) — inlining ~8 000 sub-tables would make this document several megabytes.

## Notes & gotchas

- `id` vs `displayId` — some NPCs render with the appearance of a different id (`displayId` attribute on `<npc>`). The wire `NpcInfo` packet carries the **template id** (`id`); the client then looks up appearance data for `displayId`. This doc lists `id`.
- `usingServerSideName="true"` → the server tells the client to pull the name from its own `.dat` files rather than the XML `name` attribute. Those rows may appear blank in the Name column.
- Non-aggressive mobs have no `<ai aggroRange>` (blank in `Aggro` column); they still retaliate when hit.
- Drop `Chance %` is already a percentage (0–100), not a 0–1 fraction or the raw 0–1 000 000 server integer. The XML file ships percentages directly.
- Receiving an unknown `npcId` in `NpcInfo` must never desync the game XOR stream: log and drop the packet, but still advance the key rotation in [game_crypt.py](../src/l2py/crypto/game_crypt.py) — the same rule as for unknown opcodes.
